 Google has deleted 22 apps from its Play Store following a blog post written by Sophos, a cyber security company that makes security apps
 ye eps kisi computer yaa mobile virus kii tarah khatarnaak the
 In these, a backdoor was created which helped fraud through advertising
 inke delit hone se pehle in 22 ko kul 20 lakh baar downlod kiya ja chukaa tha
 Sophos in its investigation found that these apps were linked to the Andr and Clickr-ad network
 security company ne likhaa ki ye ek suvyavasthit mailevyar hai jo yugers or puure android echosystem ko gaharaa nuksaan pahunchaa sakate hai
 Because these apps give good special revenue of ad network through fake clicks
 Sophos ne apane blog main vistaar se bataaya he ki ye eps kaise logon ke phones ko nuksaan ko pahunchaa sakate hai
 The company said that these apps drain the phone's battery and can also cause data overage as these apps are running continuously and communicating with the server in the background
 iske alaava chunki divaais puri tarah se C2 sarwar control main aa jaataa he aise main sarwar ke instrection par kisi bhi khatarnaak modul ko phone par install kiya ja saktaa he
 That is, in total, these 22 apps should not be on your phone
 philhal Sophos kii report ke baad google ne in eps ko play store se hataa diya he
 However, it is not clear whether these apps have been removed from people's smartphones or not
 agar ap play store se downlod kiye gaye hai or yugers internet se connected hai to google sidhe logon ke phone se install kiye gaye ap ko delit kar saktaa he
 This is not the first time popular apps have been named click fraud
